### [Oct 24 - Oct 30, 2022](/content/2022/43/README.md)



#### [1. Static Analysis](/content/analysis-tools-dev/static-analysis/README.md)

##### Programming Languages / [Other](#other-1)

*   [STOKE (‚≠ê643)](https://github.com/StanfordPL/stoke) ‚Äî A programming-language agnostic stochastic optimizer for the x86\_64 instruction set. It uses random search to explore the extremely high-dimensional space of all possible program transformations.
*   [CScout](https://www.spinellis.gr/cscout) ‚Äî Complexity and quality metrics for C and C preprocessor code.
*   [CSharpEssentials (‚≠ê156)](https://github.com/DustinCampbell/CSharpEssentials) ‚Äî C# Essentials is a collection of Roslyn diagnostic analyzers, code fixes and refactorings that make it easy to work with C# 6 language features.
*   [VSDiagnostics (‚≠ê64)](https://github.com/Vannevelj/VSDiagnostics) ‚Äî A collection of static analyzers based on Roslyn that integrates with VS.
*   [coffeelint](http://www.coffeelint.org) ‚Äî A style checker that helps keep CoffeeScript code clean and consistent.
*   [effective\_dart](https://pub.dev/packages/effective_dart) ‚Äî Linter rules corresponding to the guidelines in Effective Dart
*   [elm-analyse](https://stil4m.github.io/elm-analyse) ‚Äî A tool that allows you to analyse your Elm code, identify deficiencies and apply best practices.
*   [dingo-hunter (‚≠ê299)](https://github.com/nickng/dingo-hunter) ‚Äî Static analyser for finding deadlocks in Go.
*   [dupl (‚≠ê298)](https://github.com/mibk/dupl) ‚Äî Reports potentially duplicated code.
*   [lll (‚≠ê61)](https://github.com/walle/lll) ‚Äî Report long lines.
*   [safesql (‚≠ê568)](https://github.com/stripe/safesql) ‚Äî Static analysis tool for Golang that protects against SQL injections.
*   [aether](http://aetherjs.com) ‚Äî Lint, analyze, normalize, transform, sandbox, run, step through, and visualize user JavaScript, in node or the browser.
*   [es6-plato (‚≠ê201)](https://github.com/the-simian/es6-plato) ‚Äî Visualize JavaScript (ES6) source complexity.
*   [escomplex (‚≠ê251)](https://github.com/jared-stilwell/escomplex) ‚Äî Software complexity analysis of JavaScript-family abstract syntax trees.
*   [Esprima](https://esprima.org) ‚Äî ECMAScript parsing infrastructure for multipurpose analysis.
*   [luacheck (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/mpeterv/luacheck) ‚Äî A tool for linting and static analysis of Lua code.
*   [Mondrian](http://trismegiste.github.io/Mondrian) ‚Äî A set of static analysis and refactoring tools which use graph theory.
*   [PHP-Token-Reflection (‚≠ê190)](https://github.com/Andrewsville/PHP-Token-Reflection) ‚Äî Library emulating the PHP internal reflection.
*   [phpca (‚≠ê92)](https://github.com/wapmorgan/PhpCodeAnalyzer) ‚Äî Finds usage of non-built-in extensions.
*   [PhpDependencyAnalysis](https://mamuz.github.io/PhpDependencyAnalysis) ‚Äî Builds a dependency graph for a project.
*   [phpdoc-to-typehint (‚≠ê228)](https://github.com/dunglas/phpdoc-to-typehint) ‚Äî Add scalar type hints and return types to existing PHP projects using PHPDoc annotations.
*   [phpsa (‚≠ê649)](https://github.com/ovr/phpsa) ‚Äî Static analysis tool for PHP.
*   [Qafoo Quality Analyzer (‚≠ê495)](https://github.com/Qafoo/QualityAnalyzer) ‚Äî Visualizes metrics and source code.
*   [bellybutton (‚≠ê246)](https://github.com/hchasestevens/bellybutton) ‚Äî A linting engine supporting custom project-specific rules.
*   [cohesion (‚≠ê172)](https://github.com/mschwager/cohesion) ‚Äî A tool for measuring Python class cohesion.
*   [InspectorTiger (‚≠ê76)](https://github.com/thg-consulting/it) ‚Äî IT, Inspector Tiger, is a modern python code review tool / framework. It comes with bunch of pre-defined handlers which warns you about improvements and possible bugs. Beside these handlers, you can write your own or use community ones.
*   [cyclocomp (‚≠ê39)](https://github.com/MangoTheCat/cyclocomp) ‚Äî Quantifies the cyclomatic complexity of R functions / expressions.
*   [cane (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/square/cane) ‚Äî Code quality threshold checking as part of your build.
*   [Churn (‚≠ê385)](https://github.com/danmayer/churn) ‚Äî A Project to give the churn file, class, and method for a project for a given checkin. Over time the tool adds up the history of churns to give the number of times a file, class, or method is changing during the life of a project.
*   [Querly (‚≠ê241)](https://github.com/soutaro/querly) ‚Äî Pattern Based Checking Tool for Ruby.
*   [Railroader](https://railroader.org) ‚Äî An open source static analysis security vulnerability scanner for Ruby on Rails applications.
*   [Roodi (‚≠ê279)](https://github.com/roodi/roodi) ‚Äî Roodi stands for Ruby Object Oriented Design Inferometer. It parses your Ruby code and warns you about design issues you have based on the checks that it has configured.
*   [Saikuro](https://metricfu.github.io/Saikuro) ‚Äî A Ruby cyclomatic complexity analyzer.
*   [electrolysis](http://kha.github.io/electrolysis) ‚Äî A tool for formally verifying Rust programs by transpiling them into definitions in the Lean theorem prover.
*   [herbie (‚≠ê173)](https://github.com/mcarton/rust-herbie-lint) ‚Äî Adds warnings or errors to your crate when using a numerically unstable floating point expression.
*   [linter-rust (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/AtomLinter/linter-rust) ‚Äî Linting your Rust-files in Atom, using rustc and cargo.
*   [TSqlRules (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/ashleyglee/TSqlRules) ‚Äî TSQL Static Code Analysis Rules for SQL Server.
*   [linter (‚≠ê272)](https://github.com/HairyFotr/linter) ‚Äî Linter is a Scala static analysis compiler plugin which adds compile-time checks for various possible bugs, inefficiencies, and style problems.
*   [kmdr (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/ediardo/kmdr-cli) ‚Äî CLI tool for learning commands from your terminal. kmdr delivers a break down of commands with every attribute explained.

##### Other / [Other](#other-1)

*   [ciocheck (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/ContinuumIO/ciocheck) ‚Äî Linter, formatter and test suite helper. As a linter, it is a wrapper around `pep8`, `pydocstyle`, `flake8`, and `pylint`.
*   [multilint (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/adamchainz/multilint) ‚Äî A wrapper around `flake8`, `isort` and `modernize`.
*   [pure (‚≠ê223)](https://github.com/ronomon/pure) ‚Äî Pure is a static analysis file format checker that checks ZIP files for dangerous compression ratios, spec deviations, malicious archive signatures, mismatching local and central directory headers, ambiguous UTF-8 filenames, directory and symlink traversals, invalid MS-DOS dates, overlapping headers, overflow, underflow,  sparseness, accidental buffer bleeds etc.
*   [Parker (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/katiefenn/parker) ‚Äî Stylesheet analysis tool.
*   [scsslint (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/brigade/scss-lint) :warning: ‚Äî Linter for SCSS files.
*   [gixy (‚≠ê7.5k)](https://github.com/yandex/gixy) ‚Äî A tool to analyze Nginx configuration. The main goal is to prevent misconfiguration and automate flaw detection.
*   [Puppet Lint (‚≠ê767)](https://github.com/rodjek/puppet-lint) ‚Äî Check that your Puppet manifests conform to the style guide.
*   [collector (‚≠ê288)](https://github.com/banyanops/collector) ‚Äî Run arbitrary scripts inside containers, and gather useful information.
*   [Docker Label Inspector (‚≠ê79)](https://github.com/garethr/docker-label-inspector) ‚Äî Lint and validate Dockerfile labels.
*   [grunt-bootlint (‚≠ê66)](https://github.com/twbs/grunt-bootlint) ‚Äî A Grunt wrapper for [Bootlint (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/twbs/bootlint), the HTML linter for Bootstrap projects.
*   [gulp-bootlint (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/tschortsch/gulp-bootlint) ‚Äî A gulp wrapper for [Bootlint (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/twbs/bootlint), the HTML linter for Bootstrap projects.
*   [android-lint-summary](https://passy.github.io/android-lint-summary) ‚Äî Combines lint errors of multiple projects into one output, check lint results of multiple sub-projects at once.
*   [paprika (‚≠ê69)](https://github.com/GeoffreyHecht/paprika) ‚Äî A toolkit to detect some code smells in analyzed Android applications.
*   [qark (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/linkedin/qark) ‚Äî Tool to look for several security related Android application vulnerabilities.
*   [solhint](https://protofire.github.io/solhint) ‚Äî Solhint is an open source project created by <https://protofire.io>. Its goal is to provide a linting utility for Solidity code.

##### Multiple languages / [Other](#other-1)

*   [Atom-Beautify](https://atom.io/packages/atom-beautify) ‚Äî Beautify HTML, CSS, JavaScript, PHP, Python, Ruby, Java, C, C++, C#, Objective-C, CoffeeScript, TypeScript, Coldfusion, SQL, and more in Atom editor.

#### [28. Awesome Board Games](/content/edm00se/awesome-board-games/README.md)

##### Strategy

### [Talisman](https://boardgamegeek.com/boardgame/714/talisman)

> Talisman takes you on a journey through magical lands, as you endeavor to reclaim the Crown of Command.
> Each turn will see your hero advancing, battling, gaining knowledge and power necessary to defeat the guardians lurking between the Portal of Power and the Valley of Fire.

![Talisman](https://cf.geekdo-images.com/GfXN7KP7ny2YU7A-zrZObA__itemrep/img/qTes0WV8umHK5pLuKl5tZFpGYrU=/fit-in/246x300/filters:strip_icc\(\)/pic818904.jpg)

| Players | Min. Age |    Time |
| ------: | -------: | ------: |
|    2 -6 |        9 | 90-240m |
### [Pax Viking](https://boardgamegeek.com/boardgame/303954/pax-viking)

> Pax Viking is a card driven game where you compete over cards in a common market in combination with strategic movement of longships on the map. You can play cards you buy on map locations you control through your longships; create trading posts, claim benefits from events and more. You can also play cards on your jarlboard, adding abilities to your player through friends, allies and gods. Through your actions you collect followers to give you power and influence for your final bid: to be the first king of Sweden.

![Pax Viking image](https://spieltraum-shop.de/media/image/a3/40/05/show-id-1619527818652747_200x200.jpg)

| Players | Min. Age |     Time |
| ------: | -------: | -------: |
|   1 - 6 |       12 | 60 - 90m |

##### Party

### [Dune: Imperium](https://boardgamegeek.com/boardgame/316554/dune-imperium)

> Dune: Imperium uses deck-building to add a hidden-information angle to traditional worker placement. You start with a unique leader card, as well as a deck identical to those of your opponents. As you acquire cards and build your deck, your choices will define your strengths and weaknesses. Cards allow you to send your Agents to certain spaces on the game board, so how your deck evolves affects your strategy.

![Dune: Imperium image](https://ccdn.anyfinder.eu/assets/cQK9Bx79FSvDbwJQhJtnr5k7StyaUhOq7rBH00sbLEu0SSLFQQ8FcMoHNQMT36cf?height=200)

| ------: | -------: | ------: |
|   1 - 4 |       14 | 60-120m |
### [Muse](https://boardgamegeek.com/boardgame/234396/muse)

> Muse is a competitive or cooperative party game where you use imaginative clues to inspire your teammates to get them to correctly guess the Masterpiece.
> As a Muse, you need to be creative to give the right clue to lead your team to their Masterpiece. As artists, you work alongside one another to decipher that clue, and correctly choose the Masterpiece from the line-up.

![Muse image](https://cf.geekdo-images.com/6gDD73LSCMrr7ab1LHCXCg__itemrep/img/8JT5XGPKSWOt3VUGpjmfdkrBeSc=/fit-in/246x300/filters:strip_icc\(\)/pic3719954.jpg)

| Players | Min. Age | Time |
| ------: | -------: | ---: |
|  2 - 12 |       10 |  30m |
### [Jackal](https://boardgamegeek.com/boardgame/42702/jackal)

> In Jackal the players take command of pirate bands disembarking on Treasure Island. Each player may move their selected pirate once per round. The players explore the island in search of treasure to load on board their ships, while trying to recapture treasure from each other at the same time. The object of the game is to load more gold onto your ship than any other player.

![Jackal image](https://cf.geekdo-images.com/LmNDNw-RdbcQzntcfQjmoQ__itemrep/img/kJZf7177r0fj_W9RmzJdX9t_3Cc=/fit-in/246x300/filters:strip_icc\(\)/pic1638334.jpg)

### [OctoPermalinker (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/josephfrazier/octopermalinker) <a href="https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/octopermalinker/bcnkgcoohaaaclieohdlkphgfinkgbfm"><img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/alrra/browser-logos/master/src/chrome/chrome_48x48.png" width="24" /></a>

OctoPermalinker is a browser extension that searches GitHub comments/files for links to files on branches, and adds a link to where the branch pointed when the comment/file was made/updated. This helps you avoid following a link that was broken after being posted. For context, here's some discussion about broken GitHub links: [Don't link to line numbers in GitHub](https://news.ycombinator.com/item?id=8046710).

For example, suppose you're looking at a gist that links to a file on the master branch of a repo. At the time the gist was made, the link worked, but if the file gets removed, the link is broken. OctoPermalinker uses the gist creation date to add a permalink that still works.

Installs: 170 | Stars: 18 | Last update: 20 May 2017

#### [52. Awesome Asyncio](/content/timofurrer/awesome-asyncio/README.md)

##### Web Frameworks

*   [Quart (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/pallets/quart) - An asyncio web microframework with the same API as Flask.

##### Database Drivers

*   [Prisma Client Python (‚≠ê838)](https://github.com/RobertCraigie/prisma-client-py) - An auto-generated, fully type safe ORM powered by Pydantic and tailored specifically for your schema - supports SQLite, PostgreSQL, MySQL, MongoDB, MariaDB and more.

##### Networking

*   [aioping (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/stellarbit/aioping) - Fast asyncio implementation of ICMP (ping) protocol.

##### GraphQL

*   [Strawberry](https://strawberry.rocks) - Code-first Python 3 GraphQL server with Django, Flask and FastAPI/Starlette support.

##### Misc

*   [kubernetes\_asyncio (‚≠ê241)](https://github.com/tomplus/kubernetes_asyncio) - Asynchronous client library for Kubernetes.
*   [aiomisc (‚≠ê279)](https://github.com/aiokitchen/aiomisc) - Miscellaneous utils for `asyncio`.

##### Alternatives to asyncio

*   [AnyIO (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/agronholm/anyio) - High level asynchronous concurrency and networking framework that works on top of either trio or asyncio.

## Contribution

This repo is generated by [trackawesomelist-source](https://github.com/trackawesomelist/trackawesomelist-source), if you want to add your awesome list here, please edit [config.yml](https://github.com/trackawesomelist/trackawesomelist-source/blob/main/config.yml), and send a pull request, or just open an [issue](https://github.com/trackawesomelist/trackawesomelist-source/issues), I'll add it manually.


The doc is still under construction, if you have any question, please open an [issue](https://github.com/trackawesomelist/trackawesomelist-source/issues)
